---

excalidraw-plugin: parsed
tags: [excalidraw]

---
- Anywhere we see that there's A:B is 2:3, we can write it as A = 2x, B = 3x and A/B = 2/3.
- The ratio won't change no matter what you multiply it with. 2:3 will be 2:3 no matter what you multiply it with. 



# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
So, here we're given two ratios which both have B, but we can't just turn B into whatever we want
so, we multiply them together, not just normal multiply, we do; 


a:b = 2:3 & b:c = 5:7

so, we know b is both 3,5 so we multiply 5 with a:b and 3 with b:c

so, (2:3) * 5 and (5:7) * 3, then we get the same b at both places, that's our final answer.

C. 10:15:21  ^kSi0Ihmm
